## <a name="windows-server-2008-extended-rights"></a><span data-ttu-id="47ba3-1529">Diritti estesi di Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="47ba3-1529">Windows Server 2008 Extended Rights</span></span>
